## First attempt

DNS in Google Cloud was not updated with the AWS dynamic DNS IP addresses of load balancers. These were the logs for that first run. Note that the default
`kubefed init` launches the federation controller manager without the `--v` option.

```
→ kubectl --context gke_${GCP_PROJECT}_us-west1-b_gce-us-west1 --namespace federation-system logs -f federation-controller-manager-2658143845-041lh
I0623 19:21:49.478674       1 controllermanager.go:93] v1.6.4

## After federation controller manager was restarted

The AWS DNS was updated after federation controller manager was restarted to add `--v=4`. Nothing in logs previously but after restarting with `--v=4` these were the logs:


```
→ kubectl --context gke_${GCP_PROJECT}_us-west1-b_gce-us-west1 --namespace federation-system logs -f federation-controller-manager-494604230-ssw3h
I0623 20:00:09.852754       1 controllermanager.go:93] v1.6.4
I0623 20:00:09.854106       1 controllermanager.go:159] Loading client config for cluster controller "cluster-controller"
I0623 20:00:09.855061       1 controllermanager.go:161] Running cluster controller
I0623 20:00:09.891571       1 reflector.go:198] Starting reflector *v1beta1.Cluster (0s) from k8s.io/kubernetes/federation/pkg/federation-controller/cluster/clustercontroller.go:109
I0623 20:00:09.891737       1 reflector.go:236] Listing and watching *v1beta1.Cluster from k8s.io/kubernetes/federation/pkg/federation-controller/cluster/clustercontroller.go:109
I0623 20:00:09.893481       1 interface.go:248] Default route transits interface "eth0"
I0623 20:00:09.893740       1 interface.go:93] Interface eth0 is up
I0623 20:00:09.893860       1 interface.go:138] Interface "eth0" has 2 addresses :[10.52.0.6/24 fe80::a49a:13ff:feea:f23/64].
